Mitambo yeCastle Lager Premier Soccer League ichambomiswa svondo rino ichipa mukana kumutambo we2017 Africa Cup of Nations pakati peZimbabwe neGuinea .
Mashoko atirikunzwa arikuti mutambo uyu wavekutambirwa kuRufaro Stadium kwete kuNational Sports Stadium .
Vabereki vane vana muzvikoro zvebhodhing'i vanoti vava kubvisa vana vavo muzvikoro izvi sezvo zvikoro izvi zvava kuvadhurira .
Vabereki vakataura neStudio7 mushure mekushanyira vana vavo vanoti vakaudzwa kuti mari yechikoro yakakwidzwa nezvikamu zvinopfuura zana kubva muzana zvikoro zvichinzi zviri kuti mitengo yechikafu iri kukwira zuva nezuva muzvitoro .
Ukuwo vakuru vezvikoro vanoti vave kunetseka kutengera vana vechikoro chikafu chakakwana nekuti mitengo iri kukwira zvichiita kuti mari yakabharwa nevabereki vevana ava isakwanie
Mumwe ane mwana ari pachikoro chakakwidza mari , VaOscar Makova , vanoti kuendesa mwana kubhodhing'i kwave kurwadza nekuwedzerwa kwaitwa mari idzi .
Muzvare Molly Murinye vanotiwo kunyange hazvo zvinhu zviri kukwira munyika , zvikoro zvinofanira kuziva kuti mari inotambirwa nevashandi , kunyanya vehurmende , haisi kukwira sezviri kuita mitengo yezvinhu muzvitoro .
Studio7 haina kukwanisa kubata mukuru wemabasa mubazi rezvedzidzo yepasi mudunhu re Masvingo , VaZedius Chitiga , kuti tinzwe pamire hurumende .
Asi mutevedzeri wegurukota rezvidzidzo yepasi , VaEdgar Moyo , vanoti hurumende yakapa mvumo kuzvikoro kuti zviwirirane nevabereki pakukwidzwa kwe mari dzechikoro vozonyora tsamba yekupiwa mvumo kubazi ravo .
Asi mumwe mubereki , Muzvare Sungano Zvarebwanashe , vanoti sezvo kukwidzwa kwakatendedzwa nehurumende , vanoona zviri nani kudzosa vana vavo vadzidze havo pazvikoro zvavanenge vachibva kumba , izvo zvisiri kuwedzera mari nekuti hakutengwi chikafu .
Muzvikoro zvizhinji , vadzidz vanoti vave kushuva nyama sezvo yave kudhura izvo zviri kuita kuti vadye nemuriwo wekabeji , bhinzi kana mukaka .
Vadzidzi ava vanotiwo mangwanani vari kudya bota chete sezvo chingwa chave kudhura zvakanyanya .
Mumwe mubereki , VaTakunda Mutengwa , vati zvinhu zvikaramba zvakadai vana vanogona kurwara nezvirwere zvekushaiwa chikafu chakakwana .
Vabereki vevana vepachikoro che Gokomere Mission vakanetsana nemusi weMugovera nevakuru vechikoro ichi pamusangano wakaitwa zuva rekushanyira vana apo vanga vanzi vawedzere mari inosvika chiuru nemazana mapfumbamwe emadhora .
Izvi zvakarambwa nevabereki avo vakati pakavhurwa kwezvikoro mwedzi wapera , vakabhadhara chiuru chemadhora nemazana maviri .
Vabereki nevakuru vechikoro ichi vakazowirirana kuti vawedzere mazana matanhatu emadhora .
Zvimwe Zvikoro zvakaita seChibi ne Dewure High zvakawedzera mari inopfuura chiuru chemadhora .
Zvikoro zvinonzi zviri kuramba zvichiwedzera mari nekuti mitengo yechikafu , nemafuta edzimotokari iri kukwira svondo roga roga .
Mutevedzeri wegurukota redzidzo yepamusoro , VaGodfrey Gandawa , vakati makoreji munyika anofanira kupinza vadzidzi vakawanda vanorarama nehurema muzvikoro izvi sezvo hurumende iri kukurudzira kuti vanhu vanorarama nehurema vadzidze pamwe nevamwe .
Vachitaura pamabiko ekupemberera vadzidzi vainge vapedza zvidzidzo pachikoro chevadzidzisi cheMasvingo Teachers College nguva pfupi yapfuura , VaGandawa vakati hurumende inoda kuona zvikoro izvi zvichiwedzera vadzidzi vane hurema .
Vakati vanofara kuti zvikoro zvakaita seMasvingo neUnited College of Education kuBulawayo zvave kutoita izvi .
Asi vakati zvikoro izvi zvinofanira kuwedzera huwandu hwevadzidzi ava uyewo zvimwe zvikoro zvevadzidzisi pamwe nemaUniversities zvinofanira kutora vadzidzi vanorarama nehurema vakawanda .
Muzvare Makanaka Gumbo vakati kurudziro yehurumende yakanaka chose sezvo vanhu vanoraramba nehurema vange vasiri kuwana mikana seinowanawo vamwe mumakoreji .
Munyori wenhau anorarama nehurema uye achishanda nevanhu vanorarama nehurema , VaPatrick Musira vakati kurudziro yehurumende yakanaka asi vakati hurumende inofanira kuona kuti makoreji aya ane zvinhu zvinoshandiswa nevanorarama nehurema kuti vakwanise kudzidza zvakanaka .
Mukuru weCentre for Disability and Development , VaMasimba Kuchera vakatiwo izvi zvakakosha asi makoreji anofanira kushandisa mari yakawanda kugadzirisa zvivakwa zvavo kuti vadzidzi vanorarama nehurema vadzidze vasina dambudziko .
Vakatiwo kurudziro chete haina kukwana vachiti kuti zvikoro zvepamusoro zvikwanise kutora vadzidzi vanorarama nehurema hurumende inotofanira kuitwa mutemo .
Munyika mune vanhu mamiriyoni maviri vanorarama nehurema uye vazhinji vevanhu ava vanoshaya mikana yekuenda kuzvikoro sezvo zvikoro zvizhinji zvepasi nezvepamusoro zvisina dzimba dzekudzidzira nemimwe midziyo inoita kuti vanhu ava vadzidze zvakanaka .
Vanhu vakawanda vari kuswera vari mumitsetse nemotokari dzavo vakamirira kuwana peturu mumagaraji akawanda .
Vanoshandisa motokari dzavo mukufamba vanoti panzvimbo yekuti dambudziko remafuta edzimotokari rigadzirike , zvinhu zviri kutoramba zvichishata .
VaJoseph Tanyanyiwa , avo vanga vakamirira mafuta paHigh Glen Shopping Center , vati vange vamira mumutsetse kubva na7 mangwanani uye vanga vasati vawana mafuta na 2pm dzemasikati .
VaTanyanyiwa vati munyika munofanirwa kuita hurukuro dzinobata munhu wese kuitira kuti nyika ibude mumadhaka mairi .
VaMicheck Chawatama vatiwo nhasi ranga riri zuva repiri vari mumutsetse wemafuta epeturu .
Mumwe muruume ada kuzivikanwa nezita rekuti Talent Bhachi ati zvinomushungurudza zvakanyanya kuti vari kupedza nguva yekushanda kumabasa kwavo vari pamutsetse .
VaBhachi vati izvi zvinokonzera kuti nyika isafambira mberi .
Mumwe murimi , VaGoodknows Homwe , vati kushaikwa kwemafuta kuri kukanganisa mabasa avo , sezvo zvirimwa zvavo zviri kusvika pakushata vachishaya mafuta ekuti vaunze zvirimwa zvavo kumusika muHarare kubva kuGoromonzi .
Gurukota rezvemhando dzemoto , VaFortune Chasi , vakaudza vatori venhau nezuro kuti hurumende haisi kufara nezviri kuitwa nemakambani ane marezinesi ekutengesa mafuta izvo zvavakati zviri kupa kuti veruzhinji vashaye mafuta edzimotokari kunyange hurumende ichinge yaita zvose zvinodikanwa kuti munyika muve nemafuta anokwanira veruzhinji .
Hurumende yakati ichatorera makambani aya marezenesi .
Studio7 haina kukwanisa kutaura nevemagaraji kuti tinzwe kuti seyi vasina mafuta sezvo vashandi vemugaraji aya vanga vachiti havabvumidzwe kutaura nevatori venhau .
Vamwe vanoshaya muHarare vave kupinda muna 2020 vachinyemwerera mushure mekunge kambani yeOk Zimbabwe yapa masangano anobatsira vanoshaya chikafu nezvimwe pasi pehomwe yeHarare Mayor's Cheer Fund .
Vachituara pane chimwe chitoro chavo muHarare meshure mekutambidza meya weHarare , VaHebert Gomba chikafu nezvimwe zvinhu zvekushandisa , mukuru wekambani yeOK Zimbabwe , VaAlex Siyavora , vati gore negore kambani yavo inoita izvi senzira yeku rerutsira vanoshaya panguva ino apo veruzhiinji vanenge vachifara nekupembeera nehama neshamwari .
Vati kambani yavo inoita izvi mumaguta madhorobha nenzvimbo dzese dzainoshandira senzira yekubatsira vaya vasina chekubata panguva ino .
VaGomba vatenda zvikuru makambani akaita seOK Zimbabwe ayo vati anobatsira kanzuru nechikafu nezvimwe zvekupa kune vanoshaya pamazuva eKisimusi negorezva .
Vatiwo homwe yavo yeMayor's Cheer Fund haichamirira kimisimusi chete sezvo vanhu vachitambura gore rese .
Vachitaura vakamirira musha weBoka reDonhodzo wekuHighfiled uyo unochengeta vakwegura , Amai Emilia Mkaratigwa , vatenda VaGomba neOK Zimbabwe nekuratidza rudo panguva ino vachiti chikafu chavawana chichabatsira zvikuru pamusha wavo .
Nhengo yeZimbabwe Albino Association , Emmaculate Paidamoyo Chitsunza , anoti afara nezvaitwa nehomwe yaMayor's Cheer Fund .
Mamwe masangano awana Rubatsiro nhasi anosanganisira Tose Respite Care Centre , Jairos Jiri Southerton , Wheelchair Bound neHarare Children's Home .
Homwe yeMayor's Cheer Fund , ihomwe inotambira rubatsiro runosanganisira chikafu , mbatya mari nezvimwe kubva kumakambani nemasangano akasiyana uye zvese izvi zvinozopihwa kumasangano anoriritira vanoshaya nameya weguta .
Gore rino rino homwe iyi yakatsigirwa nemari inodarika zviuru mazana maviri zvemadhora .
Nguva yeKisimisi inguva yekuzorora asi veruzhiji vanoda kutora nguva iyi kuita zvakasiyana siyana .
Kune vamwe ichange iri nguva yekushanyira hama kumaruwa mushure mekupedza gore rose mumaguta .
Kune vamwewo ichange iri nguva yekushanyira vari kuchengetwa mudzimba dzevakarasikirwa nevabereki pamwe nekuvapa ruyamuro .
Asi kune vamwe , achange ari magariro emazuva ese .
Aya ndiwo mararamiro achange achiitawo vezvemitambo panguva yezororo yeKisimisi rino .

Muzvare Mguni vanoti mushure mekumhanya mhanya gore rose , ino yave nguva yekuzorora .
Muzvare Mguni vanoti vari munzira kuenda kumusha kwavo kuChimanimai kunopemberera kisimisi nemhuri yavo yese kusanganisira vamwe vari kubva kunze kwenyika .

Asi mutambi wetsiva ane mukurumbira , Charles Manyuchi , uyo ane bhande resirivha reWorld Boxing Council muhuremu hwe welterweight , anoti kwaari haisi nguva yekuzorora .
Manyuchi anoti panguva ino achange achigadzirira zvakasimba sezvo ari kutarisira mutambo mukuru gore rinotevera apo ari kurwa naDanny Garcia wekuAmerica uyo ane bhande reWBC regoridhe .
Asi maneja waManyuchi , VaChris Malunga , avo vanove zvekare mukuru weOriental Boxing Promotions , vanoti vachatora nguva ino nevatambi vavo kushanyira nzvimbo dzinochengeterwa vakarasikirwa nevabereki vachivapawo ruyamuro rwavanokwanisa .
Munyori mukuru weZimbabwe Volleyball Association , VaRingisai Mapondera , vanoti hapana chinodarika mutambo wevolleyball paKisimisi .
VaMapondera vanoti vachange vakaungana nehama neshamwari pamba pavo muHarare vachitamba mutambo uyu mukupemberera kwavo nguva ino .
Vezvemitambo vari kupinda muzororo iri panguva iyo zvinhu zvisina kumira zvakanaka munyaya dzemari , dambudziko riri kuratidza kuti hurumende iri kukundikana kuri gadzirisa .
Mapurisa nemasoja aswera achirambidza vanhu kupinda mukati meguta reBulawayo uye kudzinga vamwe vanhu vanga vave muguta nechekare .
Vamwe vanhu vataura neStudio7 vati vanetseka kusvika kumabasa kwavo sezvo mapurisa achishanda nevechiuto , ange akaisa maroadblock mumigwagwa yose inopinda mudhorobha achidzorera vanhu vakwanda kudzimba .
Mumwe mugari uyo angozvidoma nezita rekuti Sisa , uyo anogara mumusha weCowdray Park achitengesa mune chimwe chitoro chinotengesa zvekudya , ati azokwanisa hake kusvika kubasa kwake asi zvange zvakaoma .
Mumwezve mugari uyo angozvidoma nezita rekuti Amai Dube , ati ashamisika nekuona mapurisa nemasoja vachidzinga vanhu mudhorobha zvisinei nekuti mitemo yelockdown yakati zvitoro nemamwe mabhizimisi zvinogona kuvhura kusvika panguva dza3 masikati .
Mumazuva mashoma apfuura dare repamusoro reHigh Court rakapa mutongo wekuti mapurisa haana mvumo yekubvunza vanhu magwaro ekufambisa kana kuvarambidza kufamba , mushure mekunge rimwe gweta rinorwira kodzero dzevanhu , VaObey Shava , vakwira kudare nechikumbiro chechimbi - chimbi chekuti mapurisa asaite izvi .
VaShava vati vanoshushikana zvikuru nekusatevedzera mutemo kuri kuitwa nemapurisa .
Pave nemazuva akawanda mapurisa nevechiuto vachirambidza veruzhinji kupinda mumadhorobha munzvimbo dzakasiyana - siyana munyika uye vakawanda vanoti izvi zvine chekuita nekuedza kudzivirira kuratidzira kwakarongwa kuitwa mangwana .
Hatina kukwanisa kunzwa kubva kumutauriri wemapurisa , Assistant Commissioner Paul Nyathi , sezvo nharembozha yavo yange isingabatiki .
Asi mukuru wemapurisa , VaGodwin Matanga , vakaudza Studio7 neChitatu kuti kuratidzira kuri kuda kuitwa nemusi weChishanu hakuzi pamutemo uye vanhu vasina mvumo yekupinda mumadhorobha vanofanirwa kugara kudzimba dzavo .
Mune imwewo nyaya , mukuru weNational Aids Council mudunhu reBulawayo , Amai Sinatra Nyathi , vaudza Studio7 kuti veruzhinji munyika havasi kutambira zvizere kuti chirwere cheCovid - 19 chiriko uye vayambira kuti vanhu vanofanirwa kutevedzera zvinotaurwa nenyanzvi dzezvehutano senzira yekuzvidzivirira pakubata chirwere ichi .
Amai Sinatra vataura izvi mushure mekupa rubatsiro rwezvinhu zvinoshandiswa mukudzivirira chirwere cheCovid - 19 zvakaita sema Personal Protective Equipment nema sanitiser kukanzuru yeBulawayo .
Vati vaona zvakakosha kupa rubatsiro urwu sezvo vashandi vezvehutano kunyanya vana mukoti vari ivo vari panjodzi yakakura yekubatwa nechirwere cheCovid - 19 .
Pachiitiko chimwe chete sangano reWorld Vision rapawo rubatsiro kukanzuru yeBulawayo rwematangi emvura , mushonga inoshandiswa pakuchenesa nzvimbo uyewo zvipfeko nezvinhu zvinoshandiswa kudzivirira kubata chirwere ichi .
Kune vanhu gumi nevanomwe vafa nechirwere cheCovid - 19 kusvika pari zvino muguta reBulawayo uye pari zvino guta iri ndiro rine huwandu hwakakura hwevanhu vafa nechirwere ichi munyika mose .
Vamwe vana vepachikoro cheNjube High School muguta reBulawayo varatidzira nhasi vachiti havasi kufara nekukwidzwa kwemari yechikoro vachitiwo havasi kudzidza szevo vadzidzisi vakawanda vari kuramwa mabasa .
Vamwe vaona zvichiitika vati vana ava vafamba kubva pachikoro kusvika mumugwagwa weLuveve Road vachibva vazodzorerwa kuchikoro nemapurisa .
Pasvika Studio 7 pachikoro apa vadzidzi vose vange vaunganidzwa nemapurisa vachivabvunzurudza nezvikonzero zvekuratidzira .
Vana vanosvika zana avo vabvuma kuti vange vapinda mukuratidzira uku vazopinzwa mune imwe imba yekudzidzira umo vanzi vanyore zvichemo zvavo vakazonzi vanyorewo mazita avo pasi .
Mumwe mukuru wezvedzidzo kana kuti District Schools Inspector muBulawayo Amai Zanele Muyambo vaudza vana avo kuti havafanirwe kutyira kuti vachashungurudzwa .
Vati zvichemo zvavo zvinokwanisa kugadziriswa nekukasika zvichagadziriswa .
"""" Kana paine zvichemo zvamunazvo , ngatiregei kutanga taita zvekupinda mumugwagwa nekuti zvinoshatisa chimiro chechikoro chenyu , """" vanodaro Amai Muyambo .
Vaenderera mberi vachiti , """" Kutaura kwandiri kuita kudai ndinoziva kuti inzwi renyu ranzwikwa sezvamange muchida .
Asi zvakadaro chimiro chenyuwo chakanganisika .
Tine nzira dzedu dzekuti vanhu vataure nadzo , ngatidzishandisei kuti titaure zvinenge zvatinetsa . """"
Pane mashoko ekuti mumwe mudzidzisi wepachikoro ichi ndiye akurudzira kuti vana ava varatidzire asi pataedza kunzwisisa nezvenyaya iyi zvizere mukuru wechikoro uyo angozviti anonzi Msimanga ati haabvumidzwe kutaura nevatapi venhau .
Mumwe mudzidzi atisingakwanise kudoma nezita kana kubudisa pamhepo senzira yekumuchengetedza audza Studio 7 kuti vadzidzisi varatidzira pachavo vega senzira yekusafara kwavo nekukwidzwa kwakaitwa mari yechikoro uyewo kuti vadzidzisi havazi kuita basa ravo nemazvo nekuda kwekuti havazi kuwana mari yemihoro yakakwana .
Mumwe mubereki ati anonzi Amai Mudzimba atsutsumwawo nekukwidzwa kwakaitwa mari yechikoro pachikoro apa kubva pamadhora makumi mapfumbamwe kusvika pamadhora mazana mana nemakumi mana .
Amai Mudzimba vati hurumende inofanirwa kugadzirisa zvichemo zvevadzidzisi kuitira kuti zvinhu zvifambe zvakanaka munyaya yedzidzo munyika .
Zvichakadaro , VaObert Masaraure mutungamiri weAmalagamated Rural Teachers' Union of Zimbabwe , ARTUZ , vanoti zvinhu hazvina kumira zvakanaka muzvikoro kunyanya zvekumamisha uko vanoti vadzidzisi vakawanda havana kudzokera kumabasa .
Hurumende yakazivisa munguva pfupi yapfuura kuti iri kuwedzera vashandi vayo mari yemuhoro nezvikamu makumi mapfumbamwe nezvinomwe kubva muzana asi sangano reARTUZ nemamwe anoti Zimta neProgressive Teachers """" Union of Zimbabwe , akati mari iyi ishoma zvikuru sezvo zvinhu zviri kudhura zvakanyanya munyika .
Gurukota rezvemari Muzvinafundo Mthuli Ncube vakatiwo hurumende ine chido chekuda kuramba ichiita hurukuro nevashandi vayo vamwe vacho vave kuramwa mabasa vachiti havana zvikawinisiro .
Hatina kukwanisa kubata gurukota rezvedzidzo VaCain Mathema sezvo nharembozha yavo yange isiri kudairwa .
Imwe nyanzvi munyaya dzekugadzirwa kwemishona mubazi rezvehutano inoti Zimbabwe hasati yaita tsvagiridzo inoburitsa humbowo hwunoratidza kuti mbanje inogona kushandiswa semushonga unogona kurapa zvirwere zvakasiyana siyana kunyange hazvo hurumende yakadzika mutemo unobvumidza kurimwa kwembanje yekugadzirisa mishonga yakasiyana siyana .
Mukuru anoona nezvekugadzirwa kwemishonga mubazi rehutano , Amai Ropafadzai Hove , vanoti Zimbabwe haisati yaita tsagiridzo inoburitsa pachena kuti mbanje inoshanda semushonga wokurapa zvirwere zvakasiyana siyana , kunyange hazvo mbanje yava kubvumidzwa kurimwa zviri pamutemo nevanhu vanenge vapihwa marezenisi ekuita izvi .
Amai Hove vanoti mutemo uripo unoti mbanje iyi inotanga yaitwa mishonga yemafuta nemapiritsi yotengeserwa nyika dzine mitemo inobvumidza kushandisa mbanje semushonga , kwete kuitengesa muZimbabwe .
Amai Hove vanoti hurumende haisi kubvumidza munhu wese wese kuti arime mbanje sezvo ichityira kuti inoguma yoshandiswa zvisiri pamutemo .
Amai Hove vanoti kuti munhu apihwe rezenisi rekurima mbanje , anofanirwa kutanga aratidza humbowo hwekuti kune makambani ekunze kwenyika anoda kutenga mishonga inogadzirwa kubva mumbanje .
Imwe nyanzvi munyaya dzembanje , Dr Zorodzai Maroveke , vanoti danho rehurumende rekupa vanhu marezenisi harisi kutambirwa nevakawanda vagara vachishandisa mbanje muchivanhu semushonga unorapa .
Doctor Maroveke vanoti mbanje yagara ichishandiswa munyika chirungu chisati chauya .
Asi Dr Maroveke vanoti kunyange hazvo Zimbabwe iri kuomesa musoro panyaya yekuisa mitemo yembanje iyi , kune vamwe vari kutenga mishonga iyi zvisiri pamutemo kunze kwekunze izvo zviri kupa kuti nyika irasikirwe nemari yakawanda inofanirwa kuge ichivaka hupfumi hwenyika , dai Zimbabwe ichibvumidza kuti mishonga iyi itengeswe munyika .
Nyika dzakawanda dzakabudirira , kusanganisira America , dziri kushandisa mushonga unogadzirwa kubva mumbanje mukurapa marwadzo nezvimwe zvirwere zvinobata mitezo .

National Academies of Sciencies rakatambira makore maviri apfuura kuti ichokwadi kuti mishonga inobva mumbanje inogona zvikuru kupedza marwadzo muvanhu vakuru .
Kambani yeWaters Corp yekuAmerica inonzi yakapa bazi rehutano mushina unokosha madhora ekuAmerica zviuru mazana mashanu , munguva pfupi yapfuura .
Mushina uyu uchashandiswa pakugadzirwa mishonga yembanje uye mukuita ongororo yemishonga yakasiyana siyana muZimbabwe .
Pamusangano wakaitirwa kuVictoria Falls gore rino , nyanzvi dzakabva kuLiberia , Rwanda , Uganda nedzimwe nyika dzemuAfrica , dzakaratidza chido chekuda kunzwisisa mashandiro anoita mbanje semushonga .
Gurukota rezvekuburitswa kwemashoko , Amai Monica Mutsvangwa , vakazivisa kutanga kwemwedzi uno kuti Zimbabwe ichavandudza mitemo inorambidza kurimwa kwembanje , kuitira kuti vanhu nemakambani ari kupihwa marezenisi , vachitanga kurima mbanje iyi zviri pamutemo .
Pari zvino munhu anorima mbanje , kana kuwanikwa ainayo , anogona kutongerwa kugara mujeri kwemakore anosvika gumi nemaviri .
Kusaenda kubasa kwavanachiremba kwave kupararira kuzvipatara zvakawanda munyika sezvo pasina nhaurirano dziri kuitwa nehurumende kugadzirisa nyaya iyi .
Izvi zvasiya varwere vakawanda vachitambura nekushaya vanobatsira .
Vamwe vataura neStudio7 vati vari kutora nguva yakawanda vakamirira kubatsirwa vamwe vachinzi vazodzoke kana zvinhu zvave nani .
Vanachiremba vanoti vari kuda kuti mari dzavanotambiriswa dziiswe pachikero chimwe chete nemari yekuAmerica pakutengwa kwainoitwa mumabhanga pazuva zvichienzaniswa nemari yemaRTGS Dollars .
Hurumende yakawedzera vashandi vayo vemuzvipatara mari inosvika zvikamu makumi matanhatu kubva muzana svondo rapera .
Asi vashandi vakati vari kutambira asi vaine zvinyunyuto .
Sachigaro wesangano rinoona nezvevashandi mubazi rezvehutano kana kuti Health Services Board , Dr Paulinus Sikhosana , vaudza Studio7 kuti vanonzwisisa zvichemo zvavanachiremba asi vaisafanira kuramwa mabasa sezvo vati vange vaendesa zvimwe zvichemo zvavo kubazi rezvemari .
Asi mutungamiri weZimbabwe Hospital Doctors Association , Dr Peter Magombeyi , vanoti zvinhu hazvina kumira zvakanaka muzvipatara .
Dr Magombeyi vanoti vari kuda kuti hurumende igadzirise zvichemo sezvo sezvo mitengo yezvinhu yakwira zvakanyanya , kusanganisira mari dzekufambisa kuenda kumabasa avo .
Dr Magombeyi vanoti sangano ravo harisi kuramwa kuita basa asi kuti havana mari yekuti vakwanise kuenda kumabasa .
Nyaya yekudzimwa dzimwa kwemagets ichamboenderera mberi sezvo musangano pakati pehurumende yeZimbabwe neSouth Africa panyaya yekuti Zimbabwe ikwereteswe mamwe magetsi nenyika iyi wange uchifanira kuitwa svondo rino wambomira sezvo kwave negurukota idzva rezvemando dzemoto kuSouth Africa rati rinoda kanguva kekumbofema .
VaGwede Mantashe ndivo vave gurukota rezviwanikwa nemhando dzemoto .
ZESA ine chikwereti kuMozambique neSouth Africa chinosvika mamiriyoni makumi masere emadhora uye Reserve Bank of Zimbabwe iri kuyedza kubatsira ZESA kuti ibhadhare imwe mari pachikwereti ichi .
ESKOM yakati yambomira kutengesera ZESA magetsi nenyaya yechikwereti ichi .
Asi gurukota rezvemhando dzemoto , VaFortune Chasi , vaudza Studio 7 kuti vari kuti nyika dziri mudunhu reSADC dzinodzimurana ndebvu kana paita dambudziko .
Ukuwo kambani yeZimbabwe Electricity Transmission and Distribution Company iri pasi peZESA inoti makurukota ehurumende , makanzuru , mapazi ehurumende nevanhuwo zvavo vane chikwereti chakakura kuZesa chavarikutadza kubhadhara .
Zvichakadaro , VaChasi vadzingawo basa bhodhi reZESA rakadomwa musi wa 20 Kurume nevaive gurukota vebazi ravo , VaJoram Gumbo .
Vadzingwa basa vanosanganisa sachigaro VaCollins Chihuri , Muzvare Jacqueline Sande , VaTrust Chifamba , VaHussein Omar , Amai Cathrine Befura , VaThomas Timire uye Engineer Benson Munyaradzi .
Sangano reUnited Nations rinoona nezvechikafu pasi rose , reWorld Food Program , kana kuti WFP , rinoti veruzhinji vanogona kuziya nenzara munzvimbo dzakawanda munyika kana rikashaya mari rariri kuda kupa vanhu ava chikafu .
Vachitaura nevatori venhau muHarare , mutevedzeri wemukuru weWFP , kana kuti Assistant Executive Director , Muzvare Valerie Guarneri , avo vanga vachishanya munyika , vati vanhu vakawanda munyika vakatarisana nenzara yakakomba sezvo mvura isina kunaya zvakanaka mwaka uno , kubudikidza nekushanduka kwemamiriro ekunze .
Muzvare Guarneri vati sangano ravo riri kushoterwa nemari inodarika mamiriyoni zana emadhora ekuAmerica kuitira kuti rikwanise kupa chikafu vanhu vakatarisana nedambudziko renzara , zvikurusei kumaruwa .
Muzvare Guarneri vati kunyange WFP iri kubatsira mhuri dzemudhorobha dziri kutambudzika nemari yekuti dzitenge chikafu , chave kunetsa ndechekuti kuti zvinhu zviri kukwira mitengo zuva nezuva zvave kuita kuti mari yavari kupa vanhu ava kuti vabatsirikane , isakwane kutenga zvakawanda .
WFP iri kupa madhora ekuAmerica mapfumbamwe pamunhu mumadhorobha pavanhu vanenge vaonekwa kuti havakwanise kuzviraramisa .
Mumiriri weWFP muZimbabwe , VaEddie Rowe , vati kana vemasangano anobatsira pamwe nevanhuwo zvavo vakakwanisa kuvapa mari yavari kuda , vanogona kusvitsa chikafu kuvanhu mamiriyoni mana nezviuru zana kusvika vanhu vakohwa .
Vanhu vanosvika mamiriyoni manomwe nemazana manomwe ezviuru vanoda rubatsiro rwechikafu muZimbabwe .
Pavanhu vari kukwanisa kubatsirwa nechikafu neWFP munyika yose , panosera paine mamiriyoni matatu nemazana matanhatu ezviuru vanofanirwa kunge vachibatsirwa nechikafu nehurumende pamwe nemamwe masangano anobatsira asiri WFP .
Gurukota rezvekurima , VaPerrance Shiri , vati sezvo mvura isiri kunaya zvakanaka zvinoita kuti nyika ive nenzara , varimi vanofanira kurima mbesa dzisingade mvura yakawanda kuitira kuti vagokwanisa kukohwa .
Asi mumiriri weNorton muparamende , VaTemba Mliswa , vati hurumende inofanira kubhadhara varimi zvakafanira zvinoita kuti vaite basa ravo nemazvo kuitira kuti vanhu vasaziye nenzara .
Nyanzvi munyaya dzekurima dzinoti Zimbabwe haisati yambotarisana nenzara yakaita seye rwendo rwuno , uye dzinotarisira kuti huwandu hwevanhu vachada rubatsiro gore rino huchakwira kudarika pahuri pari zvino sezvo vanhu vakawanda vachatadza kuita goho rakanaka .
Hurumende iri kukurudzira veruzhinji kuti vatenge chikafu chakauchikwa kuitira kuti chive nechikafu chinovaka muviri izvo zvinoita kuti vanhu vave nehutano hwakanaka .
Vachitaura pamusangano wekudzidzisa mapazi ehurumende pamwe nevatapi venhu nezvechikafu chinovaka muviri , vanoona nezvekufambiswa kwemabasa munyaya dzezvekudya kune utano mubazi rezvehutano , VaDexter Chagwenya , vati vanhu vazhinji vari kudya zvikafu zvisina zvinhu zvinodiwa mukuvaka muviri .
VaChagwenda vanoti kushaikwa kwezvinovaka muviri kunokonzera kuti vanhu vabatwe nezvirwere zvinokonzerwa nekushaiwa hkwezvinovaka muviri .
VaChagwenda vakurudzira kuti vanhu vadye zvikafu zvakaita sehupfu , mafuta ekubikisa , munyu negorosi zvakapamidzirwa zvikwanisiro izvi , kana kuti fortified foods .
Vati hurumende yakabvumidzamakambani anogadzira zvikafu zvakita seupfu , mafuta ekubikisa pamwe nezvinwiwa zvakaita kuti zviuchikwe kuitira kuti vanhu vawane hutano hwakakwana munyika
VaChagwenya vakurudzira madzimai pamwe nevana vadiki kuti vange vachikoshesa kuwana chikafu chakauchikwa , sezvo kazhinji vari ivo vanonyanya kusangana nedambudziko rekushomeka kwezvikwanisiro izvi mumiviri yavo , izvo zvinozoita kuti vabatwe nezvirwere zvakasiya - siyana .
Vachitaurwo pamusangano mumwe chete uyu , vanoona nezvekufambiswa kwemabasa mukugadzirwa kwembeu , kukambani yeHaverst Plus , VaSimbarashe Mudani , vati kumaruwa kune vasingakwanisi kutenga zvikafu zvakauchikwa nezvinovaka muviri , nokudaro vanhu ava vanofanirwa kutenga mbeu dzakauchikwa nechekare .
Vati mbeu idzi dzikarimwa dzinobudisa chikafu chine zvinovaka miviri yevagari vekumaruwa .
Vati varimi vanofanirwa kukoshesa kutenga mbeu yechibage , nyemba , mbatatisi nedzimwe dzakasiyana - siyana kukambani yavo sezvo ine mbeu dzakauchikwa kare .
Vanoona nezvekufambiswa kwemashoko musangano reWorld Food Programme muZimbabwe , VaTatenda Macheka , vati vatori venhau vanofanirwa kuburitsa nhau dzinobata kukosha kwekudya chikafu chine zvinovaka muviri .
Bazi rezveutano rinoti vanhu vazhinji munyika vari kudya zvikafu zvisina zvinovaka hutano nenyaya yehurombo izvo zvinokonzera kuti vabatwe nezvirwere votadza kurarama kwenguva yakareba .
Masangano eKalanga Language and Cultural Development Association remuZimbabwe pamwe nereDomboshaba Cultural Trust nuBotswana , abatana neChitatu mukukuridzira kuchengetedzwa kwerurimi urwu , pamwe netsika nemagariro evanhu vanotaura rurimi urwu .
Kwanga kuine mufaro mukuru mumusha pamuzinda weDomboshaba Ruins , uri pedyo nemusha weMasunga , uko vanhu vanga vachifara vachiimba nziyo , kutamba pamwe nekudya chikafu , pahurongwa hwabatanidza vanotaura rurimi rwe Kalanga muZimbabwe neBotswana
Vachitaura neStudio7 pamucheto pehurongwa uhwu , sachigaro weKalanga Language and Cultural Development Association , VaTshidzanani Malaba vanoti chinangwa chechirongwa ichi ndechekuchengetedza rurimi rwevaKalanga .
"""" Kalanga yeBotswana neKalanga yeZimbabwe , eeh , rurimi rwumwechete .
Ndizvo vaKalanga vekuno nevaKalanga vekuZimbabwe vari kumutsiridza rwurimi , """" VaMalaba vanodaro .
Nhengo yekomiti yevechidiki musangano iri , VaFletchers Dingimuzi Dube , avo vakadzidziswa mutauro weNdebele kuchikoro , vanoti kuremekedzwa kwerurimi urwu kwakavavhurira mikana yemabasa .
Imwe nhengo yesangano iri , Amai Lydia Maphosa , vanoti vanokurudzira vanamai rweKalanga kudzidzisa vana vavo rurimi urwu , urwo rwunotaurwa kwazvo mudunhu reBulilima muZimbabwe .
Sachigaro weDomboshaba Cultural Trust , VaKangangwani Phatshwane , vanoti vane tarisiro yekuti kushanda kwavo pamwe chete kuchabatsira kuti vagone kugutsa hurumende yeBotswana kuitira kuti itange kudzidzisa Kalanga muzvikoro zvemunyika iyi .
Chirongwa cheDomboshaba Cultural Festival chinoitwa gore rega rega muBotswana , uye chakavambwa mushure mekunge verudzi rweKalanga muZimbabwe nemuBotswana vaita chibvumirano chekukurudzira mutauro vawo , tsika nemagariro awo .
Kubva mugore ra2005 , sangano reKalanga Language and Cultural Development Association rainetsana nehurumende nechinangwa chekuti rurimi rweKalanga rwudzidziswe muzvikoro kutanga muna 2013 .
Pari zvino , Kalanga mumwe yemitauro iri mubumbiro remitemo yenyika muZimbabwe , uye rurimi urwu rwunodzidziswa muzvikoro zviri munzvimbo dzinotaura Kalanga .
Rurimi rweKalanga rwunotaurwa kwazvo munzvimbo dzinoti Plumtree , Gwanda neTsholotsho mudunhu reBulilima .
Vashandi vemumabhanga vakawanda vari kurasikirwa nemabasa zvichikonzerwa nekusamira zvakanaka kwehupfumi uye kushandiswa kwemichina yechizvino zvino .
Bhanga reFirst Capital Bank riri kugumura vanhu zana nemakumi maviri , reCommercial Bank Zimbabwe riri kutarisirwa kugumura vanhu zana ukuwo bhanga reStandard Chartered richinzi rinoda kuvhara mapazi akawanda munyika rosara nematatu chete .

Musangano mukuru weInternational Conference on AIDS and STI's In Africa , Icasa , wegumi nesere , watanga muHarare zvine mutsindo nyanzvi munyaya dze HIV / AIDS dzichizeya zviri kubuda muongororo dziri kuitwa pasi rose .
Vanoona nezvekufambiswa kwemashoko musangano reIcasa , Amai Tariro Makanga - Chikumbirike , vanoti musangano uyu uri kufamba zvakanaka uye wakaparurwa zviri pamutemo neSvondo .
Zviri kubuda kumusangano uyu zvinoratidza kuti Zimbabwe pari zvino iri kuita zvirongwa zvakanaka sechirongwa chekutora chikamu chemari yemihoro , AIDS Levy , icho chiri kukokerwa nesangano re National AIDS Councll .
"""" Zimbabwe iri kuyemurwa nezvirongwa zvainazvo pakuunganidza mari yekutsvaga mishonga yehutachiwona hwe HIV , uye sangano re UNAIDS rakakorokotedza nyika nemabasa aiyiri kuita pasi pechirongwa che AIDS Levy , """" Amai Makanga Chikumbirike vaudza Studio7 .
Dingindira regore rino rinoti """" Aids In Post 2015 : Linking Leadership , Science And Human Rights . """"
Amai Makanga - Chikumbirike vanoti nzvimbo inokwanisa kusvikwa neveruzhinji , Community Village , yaparurwa uye avo vanoda kuenda kunozeya navana mazvikokota vakasununguka kuenda sezvo pasina mubhadharo unodikanwa panzvimbo iyi .
Musangano uyu uri kuenderera mberi neChipiri panguva iyo pasi rose riri kurangarira zuva reInternational World AIDS rinorangarirwa musi wa 1 , Zvita .
Hurumende yaburitsa mazuva achatambirwa mari dzekutendwa kana kuti mabhonasi egore rino evashandi vayo vose , ichiti vari muchiuto , chipurisa pamwe nevehutano vanotambiriswa mari idzi musi wa15 Mbudzi gore rino .
Vadzidzisi vanonzi vachawaniswa mari dzavo dzemabhonasi nemusi wa17 Zvita , kuchitiwo vamwe vashandi vehurumende vese vachinzi vachatambiriswa musi wa 20 Zvita .
Mashoko aburitswa nebazi rezvekuburitswa kwemashoko anoti mushandi achapiwa bhonasi pachitariswa mari yaanotambira pamwedzi , pamwe nemari yekubaitsirika nepekugara neyekufambisa .
Studio 7 yakundikana kubata gurukota rezvekuburitswa kwemashoko , Amai Monica Mutsvangwa , sezvo vanzi vanga vari mumusangano panguva yatavafonera .
Asi sangano rinomirira vamwe vashandi vehurumende , reApex Council , rinoti harisi kufara nehurongwa hwekuti vashandi vanopatsanurwa pakupiwa bhonasi sezvo izvi zvichiomesera vachapiwa mari dzavo mwedzi unouya .
Munyori weApex Council , VaDavid dzatsunga , vanoti vashandi vachatambiriswa mari idzi muna Zvita vachadziwana dzisisina simba rekutenga zvakawanda nekuda kwe inflation .
VaDzatsunga vanoti masangano evashandi ari pasi pesangano ravo achagara pasi kuti vabude nechisungo chavangatora kuenda mberi , sezvo vambotadziswa nemapurisa kusvitsa gwaro ravo renyunyuto kugurukota rezvemari , VaMthuli Ncube .
Nhengo dzeparamende dzaungana kwenguva diki kuHarare International Conference Centre pamusangano usina kupindwa nenhengo dzeparamende dzeMDC inotungamirwa naVaNelson Chamisa .
Vachitaura pamusangano uyu , uyo usina kupindwa nenhengo dzebato guru rinopikisa reMDC , mutauriri weparamende , Advocate Jacob Mudenda , vazivisa kuti paramende ichatanga kuita basa rayo rese svondo rinouya kusanganisira kuita misangano neveruzhinji kuti inzwe pfungwa dzavo pamusoro pemabhiri ari muparamende pamwe nedzimwe nyaya dzakakosha .
VaMudenda vatiwo makomiti ese eparamende achatanga kuita basa rawo svondo rinouya pachitevedzwa gwara rekudzivirira kupararira kwehutachiona hweCoronavirus , uhwo hunokonzera chirwere cheCovid - 19 .
Vati pari zvino makomiti masere chete ari kuongorora zviri kuitwa nehurumende pamusoro pechirwere cheCovid - 19 , ndiwo chete ari kuita misangano .
Vatiwo sezvo muNational Assembly musina nzvimbo dzinokwana kuti nhengo dzedare iri dzigare dzakaparadzana kwemita imwe chete sezvinodiwa pasi pemutemo wekudzivirira Coronavirus , dzimwe nhengo dzichatevera zvinenge zvichiitika mudare dziri kunze kwedare .
VaMudenda vati zvakakosha kuti nhengo dzese dziuye nemichina yechizvino zvino kana kuti matablets adzakapihwa neparamende kuti dzikwanise kutevera zvininege zvichiitika dziri kunze kwedare asi dziri panzvimbo yadzichagadzirwa pamuzinda weparamende .
Kunyange hazvo nhengo dzeMDC dzisina kuuya kudare sezvo dziri kusafara nekudzingwa kwakatwa vamwe vadzo vana mudare iri svondo rapfuura , vanokokera nhengo dzeZanu PF mudare iri , VaPupurayi Togarepi , vati vachaenderera mberi nebasa zvisinei nekuramwa kweMDC .
MDC yakabuda nechisungo chekuti nhengo dzeparamende dzayo hadzisi kuzoenda kuparamende kunoita basa zvichitevera kudzingwa kwakaitwa Muzvare Thabitha Khumalo , VaChalton Hwende , VaProsper Mutseyami pamwe naAmai Lilian Timveos muparamende neMDC inotungamirwa naMuzvare Thokozani Khupe .
Mutemo unoti dare reNational Assembly rinokwanisa kugara nekuita basa kana paine nhengo makumi manomwe chete uye Zanu PF ine nhengo dzinodarika mazana maviri mudare iri .
Gurukota rinoona nezvemitemo neparamende , VaZiyambi Ziyambi , vati rimwe bhiri rinotarisirwa kunzikwa nechimbichimbi ibhiri rekusandura bumbiro remitemo yenyika , reConstitutional Amendment Bill No2 .

Mutungamiri wesangano revashandi , reZimbabwe Congress of Trade Unions , ZCTU , VaPeter Mutasa , vanoti neChitatu chesvondo rino vakanyorera mutungamiri wenyika , VaEmmerson Mnangagwa , tsamba vachikurudzira kuti vashevedzere musangano wechimbichimbi pakati pevashandi , vashandirwi nehurumende wekugadzirisa matambudziko akatarisana nenyika mune zveupfumi .
VaMutasa vanoti musangano uyu , weTripartite Negotiating Forum , ndiyo chete nzira inogadzirisa matambudziko akatarisana nevashandi pamwe neveruzhinji , avo vavanoti vave kutadza kuenda kumabasa kana kutenga zvekudya nekuda kwekuoma kwezvinhu .
Vanoti vakapa mutungamiri wenyika mazuva manomwe ekuti vadzoke kwavari nemhinduro inogutsa , inove yekushevedzera musangano uyu .

Asi VaMutasa vanoti havasi kumirira kunzwa mhinduro yemutungamiri wenyika kwete , sezvo vatotanga kutenderera nenyika vachinzwa pfungwa dzevanhu panyaya yekuoma kwezvinhu munyika , uye matanho angakodzera kutora kugadzirisa zvinhu
Vanoti mitengo yezvinhu zvose munyika iri kukwira zvakanyanya asi mihoro yevashandi isina kwairi kuenda .
Gurukota rezvehutano , VaObadiah Moyo , vasungwa nekomisheni inoona nezvekurwisa huori , yeZimbabwe Anti Corruption Commission , Zacc , vachipomerwa mhosva yekuita huori pakutengwa kwezvinhu zvekushandisa mukudzivirira kupararira kwechirwere cheCovid - 19 .
Mutauriri weZacc , VaJohn Makamure , vati VaMoyo vasungwa zvechokwadi uye vari kutarisirwa kumiswa pamberi pedare neMugovera .
VaMoyo vakachengetedzwa muchitokisi chepaHarare Central Police Station .
Studio7 haiana kukwanisa kubata mutauriri wemapurisa , Assistant Commissioner Paul Nyathi , kuti tinzwe zvizhinji nekusungwa kwaVaMoyo sezvo VaMakamure vasina kuburitsa mashoko akawanda .
VaMoyo igurukota rechipiri muhurumende yaVaEmmerson Mnangagwa kusukwa vari pabasa neZaac zvichitevera kusungwa Amai Prisca Mupfumira gore rapera vachipomerwa kuita zvehuori .
Kusungwa kwaVaMoyo kunotevera kusungwa svondo rapera kwemumiriri weDrax International muZimbabwe , VaDelish Nguwaya , vachipomerwa mhosva yekukorovhera hurumende pakutengwa kwezvinhu zvekushandisa mukurwisa chirwere cheCovid - 19 .
VaNguwaya vakanyimwa mukana wekubvisa mari yechibatiso vachuchisi vachiti vanogona kuvhiringidza kuferefetwa kwenyaya dzavari kupomerwa , uye kutiza munyika .
Huwandu hwevanhu vabatwa nechirwere cheCovid - 19 muZimbabwe hwakwira kusvika pazana nemakumi matatu nemaviri kana kuti 132 .
Izvi zvinotevera kubatwa kwevanhu makumi masere nevatanhatu nechirwere ichi kuBeitbridge , Harare neMasvingo nemusi weChitatu .
Munhu mumwe chete pavanhu vose ava ndiye akatapurirwa chirwere ichi munyika asi vamwe vose vakabva kuSouth Africa nedzimwe nyika .
Munyori mubazi rezvekuburitswa kwemashoko , VaNick Mangwana , vari kukurudzira vanhu kuti vasachengete hama kana shamwari dzinenge dzatiza munzvimbo dziri kuchengeterwa vanenge vabva kune dzimwe nyika ava .
Vatiwo vanhu vasabatsire vaye vanenge vapoya pamabhodha vachiti izvi zvine njodzi .
Vati vanhu vakadai vanofanira kumhan'arirwa kumapurisa .
Mashoko atumirwa Studio7 neAfrican Union achibva kuAfrica Centers for Disease Control and Prevention anoratidza kuti vanhu vanodarika zvuru zana negumi nezvipfumamwe kana kuti 119 , 000 vabatwa nechirwere cheCovid-19 muAfrica uye vashaya vadarika zvuru zvitatu nemazana mashanu ane makumi mapfumbamwe nevaviri kana kuti 3 , 592 .
Vapora vadarika zvuru makumi mana nemasere 48 , 0 .
Huwandu hwevanhu vabatwa nechirwere cheCovid-19 pasi rose hwadarika mamiriyoni mashanu nemazana manomwe ezviuru kana kuti hwadarika 5 , 7 million , uye vafa vadarika zviuru mazana matatu nemakaumi mashanu nezvishanu , kana kuti vadarika 355 , 0 .
Johns Hopkins University yemuAmerica iyo iri kuongorora kupararira kwechirwere ichi pasi rose , inoti muAmerica ndimo mune vanhu vakawandisa vabatwa nechirwere ichi avo vadarika miriyoni imwe chete nezvuru mazana manomwe kana kuti vadarika 1 , 7 million .
Vanhu vafa muAmerica vadarika zvuru zana kana kuti vadarika 100 , 000 .
Chizvarwa cheZimbabwe chinoshanda kuBritain , Dr Brighton Chireka , vaudza Studio7 kuti nzvimbo dziri kuchengeterwa vanhu dzinofanirawo kuvhenekwa kuti hadzisi idzo here dzave kutonyanya kutapurira vanhu chirwere ichi .
Sangano rinomirira vadzidzi vezvikoro zvemapamusoro , reZimbabwe National Students Union , kana kuti ZINASU , nhasi ranyorera tsamba gurukota rinoona nezvedzidzo yepamusoro , Muzvinafundo Amon Murwira , richikumbira kuita hurukuro navo pamusoro pemari yechikoro yegore rino .
Izvi zvinotevera danho rakatorwa nezvikoro zvizhinji zvemapamusoro izvo zvakatonyorera kubazi iri zvichida mvumo yekukwidza mari dzechikoro .
Mutungamiriri weZINASU , VaTakudzwa Ngadziore , vaudza Studio 7 kuti zvikoro zvave pedyo nekuvhurwa uye vanoda kuti hurumende ibude pachena pamusoro pemari ichabhadharwa nevadzidzi vemuzvikoro zvepamusoro munyika .
VaNgadziore vati kunyange hazvo VaMurwira vari kuti mari iyi haizi kuzokwidza , pane humbowo hunoratidza kuti zvikoro zvema Polytechnic nezvikoro zvinodzidzisa varairidzi zvakatokwidza mari , uye vanoona sekuti mari iyi yakakwira zvakanyanya zvekuti vabereki vakawanda havakwanisi kuibhadhara .
VaNgadziore vati sangano ravo rinoda kuti vabereki vatange vawedzerwa mari dzemihoro mari yechikoro isati yakwidzwa .
Munyori anoona nezvekuenzaniswa kwemikana pakati pevakadzi nevarume muZINASU , Muzvare Nancy Njege , vaudza Studio7 kuti vadzidzi vacharatidzira kana hurumende ikasavaterera matambudziko akatarisana nevadzidzi munyika yose .
Vaimbove munyori mukuru muZINASU , VaMakomborero Haruzivishe , vatiwo apo zvikoro izvi zviri kuvhurwa mwedzi unouya , zvakakosha kuti hurumende izivise mari dzichabhadharwa nevadzidzi kuitira kuti vatsvage mari dzechikoro paine nguva .
Vatiwo mari dziri kutaurwa muzvikoro dzakanyanyisa uye hurumende inofanira kuona zvaingaite sezvo mitengo yezvimwe zvinhu zvinodiwa mukurarama iri kugara yakakwira nguva dzose .
Zviri kunyorwa pamadandemutande zvinoratidza kuti zvidzidzidzo zvakawanda muzvikoro zvizhinji zvichange zvave kuda mari inodarika zviuru zvipfumbamwe zvemadhora pakotoro yega yega kubva pamadhora mazana matanhatu pari zvino .
Asi VaMurwira vaudza Studio7 parunhare kuti zviri kutaurwa pamadandemutande manyepo sezvo pasina mubereki angakwanise kubhara mari dziri kutaurwa idzi .
VaMurwira vabvuma kuti mari dzemuzvikoro zvepamusoro dzichakwira uye mari idzi dzichaziviswa zvikoro zvisati zvavhurwa .
Vati mari idzi dzinokwidzwa pachitevedzwa matanho , ayo vati ndiwo avari kuita pari zvino .
VaMurwira vati gore rapfuura hurumende haina kukwidza mari idzi sezvo yaida kuti zvinhu zvigadzikane munyaya dzehupfumi .
Dare repamusoro neChipiri rarasa chikumbiro chekambani yeEcoCash chekuti ribvumidze kushanda zvakare kwezviuru zvevanhu vanoita zvekufambiswa kwedzimari vachishandisa nharembozha idzo dzakanga dzavharisirwa nebhanga guru renyika , reReserve Bank of Zimbabwe , RBZ , kutanga kwemwedzi uno .
Bhanga reRBZ ranga riine fungidziro yekuti vanhu ava ndivo vari kukuchidzira musika mutema .
Richipa mutongo waro , dare repamusoro iri rati haringarambidze kushanda kwemutemo , richiti kutonga richitsigira EcoCash kunotadzisa RBZ kuita mabasa ayo sezvinobvumidzwa nemutemo .
Nyanzvi mune zveupfumi vachishanda vakazvimirira , VaMasimba Kuchera , vanoti zvanga zvagara zviri pachena kuti RBZ iri kunangana nevanofambisa dzimari kuEcoCash ava kwenguva ndefu .
Vanoti kunyange hazvo danho iri ratorwa , rasiyawo pamhene mhuri dzakawanda dzanga dzichiraramiswa nemabasa ekufambisa mari aya , sezvo vasisina mabasa .
Asi VaKuchera vanoti havaoni danho iri richigadzirisa dambudziko riri kukonzerwa nemisika mitema pakutengeswa kwemari yekunze .
Mutungamiriri wenyika yeSouth Africa VaCyril Ramaphosa nemusi weSvondo vakatora matanho akaomarara mukuyedza kurwisa pamwe nekudzivirira kupararira kwechirwere checoronavirus chatekeshera pasi rose
Vanhu makumi matanhatu nevana vabatwa nechirwere ichi munyika iyi .
VaRamaphosa vakazivisa kuti South Africa kutanga nemusi weChitatu inenge yave kuvhara mimwe miganhu yayo uyo kurambidza kushanyira kana kutambira vanhu vari kubva kunyika dzabatwa nechirwere ichi dzinosanganisira Italy , Iran , South Korea , Iran , Spain , Germany , US , Britain ne China .
Zvikoro zviri kuvharwawo musi uyu uye vanhu vari kurambidzwa kuungana kusanganisirawo kumiswa kwemitambo .
MuSouth Africa mune zvizvarwa zveZimbabwe zvakawanda zviri kubatwa mumambure ezviri kuitwa kudzivirira chirwere ichi .
VaOffice Jaka , avo vanobva kuKwekwe , vanoti vane chivimbo chekuti South Africa ichakwanisa kupedza dambudziko iri kunyange hazvo riri basa guru .
Asi va Jaka vanoti varikunyanyo shungurudzika zvikuru , nevana vavo vaviri varikuita zvidzidzo zveElectrical Engineering kuChina .
VaEmmanuel Mboti vanotiwo kunyangwe hazvo zvaitwa naVaRamaphosa zvakanaka , vichakanganisa hupfumi hwenyika yavo .
Vaenderera mberi vachiti kumiswa kwemitambo kuchakanganisa kurarama kwevakawanda .
Chimwewo chizvarwa cheZimbabwe chechidiki , chinogara muSouth Africa , VaMunyaradzi Mukanyiwa , vanoti vanowirirana nemashoko ataurwa naVaMbote .
Mutungamiri wenyika VaEmerson Mnangagwa , vanoti mupurisa nemusoja vakaonekwa vachirova munhu airatidzira svondo rapera vanofanirwa kusungwa .
VaMnangagwa vataura izvi padandemutande reTwitter mushure mekunge nhepfenyuro yeSky News yabudisa vhidhiyo yemapurisa achirova musungwa akange aine simbi mumaoko .
Mutauriri weZimbabwe Lawyers for Human Rights , VaKumbirai Mafunda , vaudza Studio 7 kuti izvi zvinhu zvagara zvichiitika munyika kwenguva refu naizvozvo vanoda kuona vanotyora kodzero dzevanhu vachisungwa , kwete kungotaura sezvo muromo usingazarirwe nerwizi .
Meya weguta reHarare , VaBernard Manyenyeni , vashanyira misha inogara vashoma yeBorrowdale neGlen Lorne , vachiona kuparadzwa kwakaitwa dzimba pamwe nemidziyo nemafashamu emvura yakanaya neChina muHarare .
Mutauriri wekanzuru yeHarare , VaMichael Chideme , vanoti dambudziko remafashamu munzvimbo idzi rakanyanya kuwedzerwa nezvidziro kana kuti majuraworo , ayo ari kuputswa nemvura owira padzimba kana pamidziyo .
VaChideme vanoti zvidziro izvi zviri kupedzisira zvavhara nzira dzaisimbofamba nemvura kare , izvo zvinozoimanikidzira kupinda mudzimba yoparadza midziyo .
Kanzuru iri kuyambirawo vagari kuti vakasike kubuda mudzimba dzavo kana vangofungidzira kuti vatarisana nenjodzi .
Mvura yakawanda iri kunaya munyika yose , izvo zvinonzi zvave kuita kuti nzizi dzakawanda dzifashukire .
Vanhu vakawanda vanonzi vari kuyeredzwawo nemvura pamwe nekurohwa nemheni .
Boka rinoona nezvemamiriro ekunze re meteorological department rakatopawo yambiro yekuti mvura yakawanda ichanaya kutanga neMugovera , richikurudzira vanhu kuti vagare vakangwarira .
Vanhu vakakuvadzwa nevakafirwa pamhirizhonga yemuna Nyamavhuvhu gore rapera mushure mesarudzo dzakaitwa vanoti hapana chavati vabatsirwa nacho nehurumende .
Vachitaura mushure mehurongwa hwaitwa nesangano reZimbabwe Human Rights NGO Forum senzira yekurangarira vakafa nevakakuvadzwa , mumwe wevanhu vakapfurwa mumhirizhonga iyi , VaLovejoy Munetsi , vati vari kurarama nebara repfuti mumuviri wavo izvo zviri kuvarwadza zvikuru .
VaMunetsi vanoti pavakasangana netsaona iyi , vaizvibvira kubasa vasinei nevairatidzira .
VaMunetsi vanoti pari zvino kuripwa kukuru kwavangada kubviswa bara riri mumuviri wavo .
Mumwe wevanhu akakuvara muna Nyamavhuvhu gore rapera , VaDzikamai Chivhanga , avo vaive mutyairi wekombi , vanoti vakakuvadzwa nebara pagumbo .
VaChivhanga vanoti kubva zvavakanovhiyiwa vachibviswa bara iri , havasati vakwanisa kudzokera kubasa .
VaChivhanga vanoti ivo nemhuri yavo vari kutochengetwawo , uye vanoshuvira kuti dai hurumende yavaripawo kuti varerukirwe nehupenyu .
Muzvare Precious Mabenga , avo vanotengesa zvinhu mumugwagwa , vanoti vakarohwa zvakaipisisa nemasoja huye vave kurarama nekumwa mapiritsi anonyaradza marwadzo .
Mukuru weZimbabwe Human Rights NGO Forum , Amai Blessing Gorejena , vanoti havasi kufara nehurumende nekusabatsira vanhu vakakuvadzwa nevakarasikirwa nehupenyu hwevadikanwi vavo pamhirizhonga yaNyamavhuvhu iyi .
Mukuru weZimbabwe Lawyers for Human Rights , Muzvare Roselyn Hanzi , vanoti zvinovashungurudza kuti mushure megore vanhu vakakuvadzwa nekufirwa , hapana ati aripwa , uye hapana kana musoja ati asungwa .
Mushure memhirizhonga iyi hurumende yakaisa komisheni yaitungamirirwa nevaimbove mutungamiri weSouth Africa , VaKgalema Motlanthe , kuti vaongorere chaive chakonzera mhirizhonga huye kuti chii chingaitwe .
Komisheni yaMotlanthe yakabuda negwaro rakakurudzira hurumende kuti vose vakavhiringwa nemhirizhonga iyi , varipwe .
Studio7 haina kukwanisa kunzwa kuti hurumende yasvika papi nenyaya yemhirizhonga yakaitwa muna Nyamavhuvhu .
Asi munyori mubazi rezvemutemo , Amai Virginia Mabhiza , vati tivanyorere mibvunzo , iyo tavapa , asi havana kupindura panguva yekuenda pamhepo .
Asi Amai Mabhiza vakamboudza vatori venhau kuti hurumende yakatotanga kuzeya nyaya dzevanhu makumi matatu nevashanu vakashaikirwa nehama dzavo , kana kukuvara pakapfurwa vanhu muna Nyamavhuvhu gore rapera kuitira kuti varipwe .
Mumhirizhonga iyi , sekutaura kwesangano re Zimbabwe Association of Doctors for Human Rights , vanhu vatanhatu vakapfurwa vakafa , uye vanhu makumi maviri nevapfumbamwe vakakuvara zvakaipisisa .
Vakafa musi uyu ndiBrian Zhuwawo , Jealous Chikandira , Challenge Tauro , Gavin Dean Charles , Ishmael Kumire naSlyvia Maphosa .

Bazi rezvekudyidzana kweZimbabwe nedzimwe nyika rinoti harina kufara nekutemerwa kwakaitwa VaSanyatwe zvirango neAmerica , uye rasvitsa nhasi nyunyuto yehurumende kumuriri weAmerica muZimbabwe , AmbassadorBrian Nichols .
Mutungamiri wenyika VaEmmerson Mnangagwa nhasi vakurudzira kuti munyika muve nerunyararo uye kuti musaitwe zvemhirizhonga vachiti hurumende yavo iri kuedza kugadzirisa matambudziko ese akatarisana nenyika .
VaMnangagwa vataura mashoko aya pamhemberero dzezuva remagamba enyika dzaitirwa paHeroes Acre muHarare .
Vachitaura pamberi pezviuru nezviuru zvevanhu vanga vari pamhemberero idzi , VaMnangagwa vati hurumende yavo iri kuziva matambudziko ari kutarisana neveruzhinji akafanana nekushayikwa kwemafuta edzimotokari , kushayikwa kwemari mumabhanga pamwe nekudzimwa dzimwa kwemagetsi nezvimwe zvakadaro .
VaMnangagwa vati hurumende yavo iri mubishi kugadzirisa matambudziko ese aya vakakurudzira kuti munyika murambe muine runyararo uye veruzhinji vasaita zvemhirizhonga .

nedare reConstitutional Court .
Murongi wemabasa muMDC VaAmos Chibaya vanoti vari kuratidzira nekuti zvinhu hazvina kumira zvakanaka munyika .

VaMatemadanda vashorawo MDC nekusauya kumhemberero dzezuva remagamba vachiti MDC haikoshese magamba uye vati bato iri rinongoda zvemhirizhonga chete .
Zvataurwa naVaMatemadanda zvatsinhirwa naVaLouis Matutu veboka revechidiki muZanu PF reYouth League avo vati vachatora matanho akasimba kudzivirira mhirizhonga pamwe nemasimba ehutungamiri hwebato ravo .

mitanhatu isati yapfuura kubvira apo akaritora zvekuti nguva yaManyuchi yekuita izvi yasvika .

VaHenry Makiwa vanove mukuru anoona nezvekufambiswa kwemashoko musangano reWorld Vision vanoti kunyange hazvo nyika yakwanisa kupinza chibage , vanoona chiri chishoma kwazvo pachitariswa huwandu hwevanhu vari kuda chikafu .
"""" Panotodiwa kuwedzerwa kwechikafu nekuti huwandu hwevanhu vari kuda chikafu huri kuramba huchikwira , """" VaMakiwa vanodaro .
Veruzhinji vanoti vari kukatyamadzwa zvikuru nekukwira kuri kuita mitengo yezvinhu munyika zvichitevera kurambidzwa kwemari dzekunze kushandiswa munyika .
Vanhu vazhinji vanoti vaifunga kuti zvakaiswa mutemo mutsva nehurumende wekushandisa mari yemunyika chete , mitengo yezvinhu yaizogadzikana , asi vari kushamisika zvikuru vachiona mitengo ichiita chamurambamhuru kukwira .
Vamwe vatengi vakaita sa Amai Chipo Murambiwa vanoti mitengo yezvinhu , kunyanya chikafu , yafuma yakaita chamuramba mhuru muzvitoro zvakaita seOK ne Pick & Pay nezvikamu zvinopfuura zana kubva muzana .
Muchitoro che OK makeyiji makumi mashanu ehupfu aiita makumi matatu emadhora eRGTS , nhasi afuma achiita zana nemadhora maviri .
Mafuta ekubikisa aiita madhora gumi nemashanu , ave kuita madhora makumi matatu , makeyiji maviri emupunga aiita madhora masere , ave kuita madhora makumi maviri nemanomwe , ukuwo keyiji yenyama yaiita madhora gumi nemashanu , yave kuita madhora makumi matatu emaRTGS .
VaJohanes Chihwani , avo vanogara mumusha we Sisk , vanoti mutemo wakaiswa uyu watovaipira .
Sachigaro weConsumer Council of Zimbabwe muMasvingo , VaProsper Muzambi , vanoti kukwira kuri kuramba kuchiita mitengo yezvinhu kunokonzera mutauro munyika .
Vatiwo vemabhizimusi vakaramba vachidai , vanokurudzira vatengi kuti varatidzire nekuti vaifunga kuti mutemo wakauya uchaita kuti zvinhu zvidzike .
VaTatenda Matumba , avo vane chitoro mudhorobha , vati vari kuramba vachikwidza mitengo nekuti vanozondotenga mari yekunze pamukoto nekuti kumabhanga haiwanikwi .
Vanoongorora nyaya dzehupfumi hwenyika vakazvimirira , VaPardon Tshuma , vanoti mutemo wakaiswa nehurumende handiwo mhinduro yedambudziko rekukwira kwezvinhu muzvitoro kana nyika isina maindasitiri anogadzira zvinhu achitengesawo kunze kwenyika .
Muzvinafundo pachikoro cheGreat Zimbabwe University , VaMunashe Shoko , vanoti mitengo ichiri kukwidzwa nekuti vatengesi vazhinji vakange vakahodha zvinhu nemari yekunze nekudaro pazvichapera mitengo ichadzikama .
Asi vamwe vanoti kuti zvinhu zvigadzikane nyika inofanira kushandisa mari yekunze yeku nyika yeAmereka kusvika zvinhu zvazonaka .
Studio 7 yakundikana kubata gurukota rezvemari , VaMthuli Ncube , avo vanonzi vari kunze kwenyika .
Asi gurukota rinoona nezvekugadzirwa kwezvinhu nekutengeserana , VaMangaliso Ndlovu , vashora zvikuru vemabhizimusi nekukwidza mitengo yezvinhu zvisina tsarukano kubva pakarambidzwa mari yekunze kushandiswa munyika svondo rino .
VaNdlovu vaudza vatori venhau pamusangano wavaita muHarare kuti hapana chikonzero chingapa kuti vemabhizimusi vakwidze mitengo yezvinhu .
Mhuri yeZimbabwe yakabatana neChitatu mukurangarira gamba renyika , Doctor Joshua Nkomo , avo vasvika makore makumi maviri nerimwe vashaya .
Doctor Nkomo vakaberekwa muna Chikumi 1917 uSemukwe Reserve kuMatabelaland South vakashaya muna 1999 .
Vakambodzidzisa kuKezi vasati vaenda kuSouth Africa kunowedzera dzidzo kunova kwavakasangana negamba rerusununguko renyika iyi , muchakabvu Nelson Mandela , nevamwe .
VaNkomo vakashanda kuRhodesian Railways uko vakatungamira kuratidzira kwevashandi muna 1948 .
Muna 1962 vakazoumba bato reZapu iro rakapatsanuka pachiumbwa Zanu PF muna 1963 .
VaNkomo vakazosungwa muna 1964 vakapedza makore gumi vari kujeri reGonakudzingwa .
Pavakabuda mujeri vakaenderera mberi nechimurenga vachitungamira mauto eZIPRA aiva pasi peZapu kusvika nyika yawana kuzvitonga kuzere .
Vakakwikwidza musarudzo dzemuna 1980 bato ravo rikakundwa neZanu PF yaitungamirwa namuchakabvu Robert Mugabe .
VaNkomo vakaitwa gurukota rezvekuchengetedzwa kwemukati menyika asi pakabva patanga kunetsana kweZanu PF neZapu .
Mushure mekusungwa kwevakuru vebato ravo vakaita saVaDumiso Dabengwa naVaLookout Masuku vachipomerwa mhosva yekuda kupidigura hurumende , Doctor Nkomo vakamanikidzwa kuenda kuhupoteri kuBritain muna 1983 kwemakore mana asi panguva iyi pakatangwa hondo yeGukurahundi kuMatabelaland neMidlands iyo yakasiya vanhu vanofungidzirwa kuti vanodarika zviuru
makumi maviri vafa .
Mauto eFifth Brigade akadzidziswa zvehondo kuNorth Korea ndiwo anopomerwa mhosva yekuponda vanhu vasina mhaka kumatunhu aya .
VaMugabe vakafa vasina kukumbira ruregerero vakati iyi yaive nguva yekupenga .
Asi muaturiri wavo kwemakore akawanda , VaGeorge Charamba , vakati hapana chekukukumbira ruregerero sezvo yaive hondo .
Gukurahundi yakapera muna 1987 pakanyoreranwa chibvumirano cheUnity Accord pakati peZanu PF neZapu .
VaNkomo vakazoitwa mutevedzeri wemutungamiri wenyika pakavandudzwa bumbiro remutemo .
Munyori mukuru mudare remakurukota , Doctor Misheck Sibanda , vati Zimbabwe inofanisa kukoshesa runyararo nekubatana sezvaikosheswa naVaNkomo .
Kunyangwe mutungamiri wenyika , VaEmmeron Mnangagwa , vakavimbisa kugadzirisa nyaya yeGukurahundi pavakatora masimba vachitsigirwa nemauto muna 2017 , kusvika pari zvino hapana chati chaitwa chinobatika .
Nyanzvi munyaya dzezvematongerwo enyika , VaJoy Mabenge , vanoti VaNkomo mucherechedzo wemunhu ainge akazvipira kubatanidza nyika .
Mutungamiri wenyika VaEmmerson Mnangagwa svondo rino vari kutarisirwa kutungamira chikwata chemapato madiki anopikisa kuChimanimani neChipinge , Manicaland kunooona kuparadzwa kwakaitwa nzvimbo iyi detumupengo kana kuti tropical cyclone Idai .
VaMnangagwa vari kuenda nevatungamiri vakaita savanna Muzvare Thokozani Khupe , Muzvinafundo Lovemore Madhuku , VaBrian Mteki nevamwe vari muchikwata chavari kuita nacho nhaurirano .
Vamwe vatungamiri vakaisa semutungamiri webato guru rinopikisa VaNelson Chamisa veMDC , Amai Joyce Mujuru , VaNoah Manyika , VaDaniel Shumba havasi muhurongwa hwavaMnangagagwa uhu .
Hurumende inoti vanhu mazana maviri nemakumi masere vakafa uye vamwe mazana matatu havasi kuzivikanwa kuti vari kupi .
Pavanhu ava makumi masere nevaviri vanonzi vakavigwa kuMozambique mushure mekuyeredzwa nemvura .
Aka ndekechipiri vamnangagwa vachishanyira nzvimbo iyi .
Kunyangwe hazvo rubatsiro rwuri kuuya kubva kumativi mana ose enyika nekunze , vamwe vagari vemunharaunda iyi vanoti havana matende , chikafu kana mvura yekunwa yakachena .
VaMadhuku vaudza Studio 7 kuti vari kuenda kechipiri asi vanotarisira kuti rwendo rwuno vachaenda kumberi pane kwavakambosvika sezvo migwagwa yaisafambika zvakanaka .
VaMadhuku vati zuva rekusimuka harisati razivuswa asi ivhiki rino .
Vabereki vane vana vane hurema hwekusanzwa kana kuti matsi vari kukurudzira bazi rezvehutano kuti rivabatsire nezvikwanisiro , kana kuti hearing aids , kuitira kuti vana vavo vakwanisewo kudzidza sevamwe vana muzvikoro pasina dambudziko .
Vabereki vakawanda vanoti kuongororwa kwevanhu vane hurema hwekusanzwa kunodhura zvokuti vazhinji vavo havakwanise kuendesa vana vavo kunaana chiremba kuti vanorapwa hurwere uhwu husati hwakomba .
Amai Tsitsi Nlabati vekuMasvingo vanoti mwana wavo , uyo anemakore mapfumbamwe , anonzwira kure mazwi anotaurwa zvokuti vakashaya mari yokutenga ma hearing aids izvo zviri kudzosera kumashure budiriro yehupenyu hwemwana wavo .
Amai Nlabati vanoti vakavimbiswa nenyanzvi munyaya dzezvehutano kuti mwana wavo aisafanira kuenda kuzvikoro zvinodzidza vana vanorarama nehurema nokuti vainge vaine chivimbo chekuti mwana aizokwanisa kuita zvakanaka kana akatengerwa ma hearing aids .
Baba Kizito Chirenje vekuMurombedzi , kwaZvimba vanoti vane dambudziko zvakare remwana wavo uyo akambotengerwa ma hearing aids neimwe hama yavo yakambogara mhiri yemakungwa asi akadimburwa dimburwa kaviri kose nevamwe vana vaida kuziva kuti chii chaaipfekera munzeve .
Baba Chirenje vanoti hama yavo yakadzoka kumusha nokudaro havachakwanisa kuwana mamwe ma hearing aid nokuti anonzi anotengwa nemari yekuAmerica iyo vasingakwanisi kuwana .
Sachigaro wekomiti inoona nezvehutano muparamende , Dr Ruth Labode , vanoti bazi rehutano harina mari yokutengera mwana wese mahearing aids nokudaro vabereki ava vanofanira kubatsirwa nemadhona ayo anopemha mari kunze kwenyika .
Dr Labode vanoti hurumende yakaomerwa panguva ino zvokuti iri kutoshayawo mari yokutenga mishonga ine mitengo iri pasi pasi inofanira kubatsira varwere muzvipatara .
Nyanzvi munyaya dzemutauro wemaoko mubazi rezvehutano , Amai Cecilia Nleya , vanoti pane chirongwa chokuti mwana wese anozvarwa atange kuongororwa kana paine hurema waanenge ainahwo kuitira kuti vazokwanisa kubatsira vana ava pavanenge vachikura zvinoenderana nekuremara kwavo .
Asi Dr Labode vanoti kunyangwe hazvo vana ivava kana vawanikwa vaine hurema hwakadaro , hapana zvakanyanya zvinokwanisika kuitwa kuvana ava nokuti mamiriro ehupfumi hwenyika haana kumira zvakanaka .
Tsvagurudzo yakaitwa nebazi rehutano inoratidza kuti pavanhu miriyoni imwe chete yevanhu vanorarama nehurema hwakasiyana siyana , pakaonekwa kuti vanhu zviuri zana nemakumi maviri , vanhu vasinganzwe kana kutaura .
Zimbabwe yakasaina chibvumirano cheUnited Nations Conventions on the Rights of Persons with Disabilities mugore 2013 , asi nyanzvi munyaya dzemitemo pamwe nehutano dzinoti zviga zveUnited Nations izvi hazvisati zvaiswa mumitemo yenyika .
Sangano rinorwira kodzero dzevanhu , reHuman Rights Watch , rinokurudzira hurumende kuti iwanise vanhu munyika mvura yakachena kuti vakwanise kurwisana necoronavirus .
Mugwaro rayo , Human Rights Watch inoti kushaikwa kwemvura yakachena kunogona kupamidzira ngozi yechirwere checoronavirus .
Mukuru weHuman Rights Watch kuchamhembe kwe Africa , VaDewa Mavhinga , vaudza Studio 7 kuti ongororo yavakaita muZimbabwe uye muHarare nenzvimbo dzakaipoteredza inoratidza kuti kana nyaya yemvura ikasakurumidza kugadziriswa ichakonzera dambudziko guru .
Asi meya weHarare , VaHerbert Gomba , vanoti hapana asingazivi kuti Harare yagara ine dambudziko remvura kubva 1990 , vachiti kanzuru yeguta reHarare , pamwe chete nehurumende , vari kuedza kugadzirisa nyaya iyi .
VaGomba vanokurudzira masangano akasiyanasiyana kuti abatsire kugadzirisa zvinhu zvinonetsa pachinhambo chekushora vari kuedza kugadzirisa zvinhu .
Sangano rinomirira vadzidzisi vekumaruwa reAmalgamated Rural Teachers Union of Zimbabwe kana kuti ARTUZ rinoti nhengo dzaro zhinji hadzina kuenda kumabasa nhasi zvichitevera kurudziro yesangano iri yekuti varairidzi vasaende kumabasa vachitsutsumwa kuhurumende nemari dzemihoro .
ARTUZ inoti nhengo dzayo dzakawanda nhasi dzaswera dzichidziya mushana kudzimba dzisiri pabasa zvichitevera kurudziro yesangano iri yekuti nhengo dzaro dziramwe mabasa kubva nhasi kusvika neChishanu nepamusana pekushomeka kwemari dzemihoro dzavari kutambiriswa nehurumende .
Sachigaro weARTUZ mudunhu reHarare , VaMunyaradzi Masiyiwa vaudza Studio 7 kuti vadzidzisi vasina kuenda kumabasa nhasi vanodarika zvikamu makumi mana kubva muzana .
Mutungamiri weARTUZ , VaObert Masaraure vatiwo vachatora matanho akasimbarara kana hurumende ikaramba yakaisa zvimiti munzeve isiri kuda kuvabhadhara nemadhora ekuAmerica .
Zvichakadai , mumwe mubereki ane mwana anodzidza pane chimwe chikoro chiri kuGoromonzi mudunhu reMashonaland East , Amai Tinotenda Kahari , vaudza Studio 7 kuti hurumende inofanira kugadzirisa nhuna dzevarairidzi nekukasika kuitira kuti vana vasarasikirwe nedzidzo .
Zvichakadai , mutungamiri werimwe sangano revadzidzisi reProgressive Teachers Union of Zimbabwe , VaTakavafira Zhou , vati nhengo dzesangano ravo dzichatangawo kuramwa mabasa svondo rinouya .
VaZhou vati sePTUZ vachataurawo nevemamwe masangano anomirira vashandi vose vehurumende kuti vaite muonerapamwe sechuma chemuzukuru .
Mutungamiri weZIMTA VaRichard Gundani vanotiwo havasi kufara nemari dzavari kutambiriswa .
Zvichakadai , gurukota rezvedzidzo , VaPaul Mavhima vaudza Studio 7 parunhare kuti homwe yehurumende yakabooka zvekuti hurumende haikwanise kubhadhara varairidzi nemari yekunze kana kuvawedzera maRTGS parizvino .
Vati zvakawanda zvine chekuita nekuwedzerwa kwemari dzemihoro yevashandi vehurumende tibvunze kugurukota rezvemari VaMthuli Ncube avo vatisina kukwanisa kubata panharembozha yavo .
Mutauriri weHealth Apex Council VaPanganai Chivese vanoti vanachiremba , vanamukoti nevamwe vashandi vehurumende vatotanga kuramwa mabasa nezuro .
Vati vashandi vakawirirana kuenda kumabasa kaviri pazuva asi vachiita zvekuchinjana .
Vayambira kuti hurumende ikasagadzirisa zvichemo zvavo havasi kuenda kubasa vose svondo rinouya .

Chirwere ichi chinonzi chakatangira muguta iri uye mune zvizvarwa zveZimbabwe zviri kudzidza muguta iri zvinodarika mazana matatu nemakumi mashanu .
Muzvare Chirima vanoti shuwiro yavo ndeyekuti pawanikwe rubatsiro rwekubatsira ivo nevamwe vadzidzi vari kutarisana nedambudziko remari yekushandisa sezvo vamwe vaisimboita mabasa ekuzviriritira vasiri kushanda pari zvino .

Kunyange hazvo dhora rekuAmerica rakamboti dererei huremu zvichienzaniswa nemari yemunyika yemaRTGS , zvinhu zvichiri kuramba zvichidhura zvakanyanya .
Ko chii chiri kupa kuti zvidai , uye mari yeRTGS icharamba iine simba here ?
Muzvinabhizimisi , uye vari nhengo yeZanu PF yakakwikwidza ikakundikana musarudzo yekutsvaga mumiriri weWarren Park muparamende , VaGilbert Muponda , vanoti zvichatora mavhiki angangosvika matanhatu kuti zvinhu zvigadzikane .
Asi imwe nyanzvi munyaya dzezvehupfumi vachidzidzisa paNelson Mandela Metropolitan University , Muzvinafundo Gift Mugano , vanoti nedanho rekudzora dhora remunyika havaona hupfumi huchigadzikana .
Vanoti pane zvakawanda zvinoda kugadziriswa dhora risati radzoka zvisingazope kuti hurumende irambe ichidhinda mari zvakazopa kuti dhora rishaye simba mumakore ekuma 2008 .
Asi VaMuponda vanoti zvinhu zvakanaka kuti nyika ishandise dhora rayo kana ichida kubudirira .
Ko chii chaizvo chakapa kuti dhora rekuAmerica rimboshaya simba mazuva apera ?
Muzvinafundo Mugano vanoti nyaya yebhanga guru renyika , reRserve Bank of Zimbabwe , RBZ , yekutora zvikwereti zvemakambani ndeimwe yakaita kuti izvi zviitike .
RBZ yakati yaizopa vemakambani mari yekuAmerica inosvika bhiriyoni imwe chete nezviuru mazana maviri pama RTGS yairi kutora .
Imwe nyanzvi munyaya dzezvehupfumi , VaVictor Bhoroma , vanoti chiri kudererdza dhora rekuAmerica inyaya yekuti vanhu vari kuda kutanga vanzwisisa kuti zvichafamba sei .
Imwe nyanzvi munyaya dzezvehupfumi vachishanda nesangano reLabour and Economic Development Research Institute of Zimbabwe , Doctor Prosper Chitambara , vanoti danho rakatorwa negurukota rezvemari , Muzvinafundo Mthuli Ncube , zvichinzi zvichabatsira vashandi hazvisi kubatsira pari zvino .
Chimwe chizvarwa chenyika , uye vari gweta rinorwira kodzero dzevanhu , VaGodfrey Mupanga , vaendesa gurukota rinoona nezvemari nebhanga guru renyika kumatare vachivapomera mhosva yekudzika zvisiri pamutemo , mutemo unoshanda kwemwedzi mitanhatu kana kuti Statutory Instrument 142 yakarambidza kushandiswa kwemari dzekunze kwenyika .
Mutewedzeri wasachigaro vebato reMDC , VaJob Sikhala , vanoti vakakwanisa kusvitsa masamanisi kudare repamusoro ekuti varipwe mari inosvika mamiriyoni matatu emadhora ekuAmerica mushure mekusungwa kwavo gore rapera vachipomerwa mhosva yekuda kubvisa mutungamiri wenyika VaEmmerson Mnangagwa pachigaro .
VaSikhala , avo vakazowanikwa nedare repamusoro kuMasvingo vasina mhosva , vanoti vakwirira kumatare gurukota rezvemukati menyika , Vakazembe Kazembe , mukuru wemapurisa Commissioner - General Godwin Matanga , pamwe nemupurisa wekudivi reLaw and Order muHarare avanoti akavashungurudza zvikuru pavaive muhusungwa , Superintendent Daniel Joseph .
VaSikhala , vanove zvakare mumiriri weZengeza West muparamende , vakatanga danho rekukwira kumatare iri gore rapera muna Nyamavhuvhu vachikwirira mapurisa pamwe naVaCain Mathema vaive gurukota rezvemukati menyika panguva iyi .
Studio 7 haina kukwanisa kunzwa kubva kuvatatu ava kana vati vatambira masamanisi aya .
Mitumbi yaVaRoy Bennett , nemudzimai wavo , Amai Heather Bennett , inonzi iri kutarisirwa kusvika muZambia svondo rinouya , uko vanonzi vanga vava kurima vari .
Shamwari yemhuri yekwaBennett , VaBrian James , vaudza Studio7 kuti mitumbi yevaviri aya ichasvikira kuZambia svondo rinouya , uko VaBennett vanga vachirima vari .
VaJames , avo vakamboita meya weMutare , vatiwo mitumbi iyi ichazoendeswa kuSouth Africa uko inotarisirwa kuvigwa .
VaBennett nemudzimai wavo vakashaya nemusi weChitatu svondo rapera mutsaona yechikopokopo chakange chakatakura vanhu vatanhatu mudunhu reNew Mexico kuAmerica .
Vanhu vashanu vakafa mutsaona iyi .
VaRegai Tsunga vaizivana naVaBennet vasati vaenda kuhupoteri kunze kwenyika .
VaTsunga vanoti VaBennett vaibatsira veruzhinji mune zvakawanda .
VaTsunga vanoti VaBennett munhu aifarira kushandira nyika yavo , uye kushaya kwake kuri kuvarwadza zvikuru .
"""" Roy akambopokana nedzimwe nhengo dzeparamende asi ari kutaura chokwadi ; saka tinoti Roy Bennett zorora murugare , """" vadaro VaTsunga .
Mutori wenhau ayiwirirana naVaBennett , Clayton Masekesa , anoti haana mashoko mazhinji asi kungoti arasikirwa nasahwira uye nemunhu aimupa mazano nguva zhinji .
"""" Eeeh tinoti rufu kutonga kwaMwari uyezve takatarisana nenguva inorema saka tinotanga nekuti ngavafambe nekuzorora murugare VaBennett .
Iniwo semutori wenhau ndakatanga kushanda naVaBennett kare ndingati kuma - late 90s and early 2000 , anga ari munhu anga ane shungu yekuti constituency yake ibudirire .
Ange ari munhu zvakare aiva ne vision achida kuti vanhu venharaunda yake vabudirire pamwe chete neManicaland yacho .
Saka ndinoti nyika yarasikirwa nekuti tange tino vimbo yekuti munhu aizobatsira pakuvaka Zimbabwe inyuwani mune remangwana , """" adaro Masekesa .
Mutauriri weMDC mudunhu kuManicaland , VaTrevor Saruwaka , vanoti vende rasiiwa naVaBennett nemudzimai wavo richanetsa kuvhara sezvo mhuri iyi yaive nerudo uye chivimbo chekubatsira mukufambira mberi kweZimbabwe itsva .
VaBennett , avo vanga vava nemakore makumi matanhatu , vakamboita sachigaro weMDC kuManicaland , uye vakaita mubati wehomwe webato iri kwemakore akawanda .
Vana chiremba navana mukoti vanoti vari mubishi rekubatsira vanhu vekuChimanimani neChipinge vakawirwa nedambudziko redutumupengo reCyclone Idai masvondo maviri apfuura .
Mumwe wevanachiremba ava , Doctor Matthew Wazara , vanoti vanhu vakawanda vari munzvimbo dzakaparadzwa nedutumupengo nemafashamu emvura , havachina mishonga yekupodza kana kunyaradza zvirwere zvinenge shuga , diabetes , ne High Blood Pressure .
Dr Wazara vanoti vanhu vakawanda vakakuvara uye vazhinji vanofanirwa kudzorerwa pamapiritsi avainwa , uye vamwe vavo vanotoda kuitwa maoparesheni , sezvo vakakuvara zvakaipisisa .
Dr Wazara vanoti vagari vanofanirwa kunwa mvura uyakachena , sezvo mvura iri munzvimbo iyi yasangana netsvina yezvitunha , mhuka izvo zvinokwanisa kukonzera zvirwere zvinofamba nemvura zvakaita semanyoka kana korera .
Pamusoro pedambudziko rekushaya mvura yakachena , Dr Wazara vanotiwo madzimai ari kusanganawo nedambudziko rekushaya zvinhu zvavanoshandisa pamazuva avo ekutevera .
Dr Wazara vanokurudzira kuti mumatunhu aya munofanirwa kuvakwa misasa yakawanda yemakiriki kuitira kuti vanhu vawane rubatsiro nekukurumidza .
Dr Wazara vanoti kune vanhu vakawanda vari kurwadziwa nezvakaitika zvokuti vachada kunyaradzwa naana mazvikokota nenyanzvi dzinoona nezvirwere zvepfungwa kuti vagamuchire tsaona dzakavawira .
Vanotiwo kune dzidziso zvakare iri kuitirwa vafundisi vemakereke akasiyana kuti vakwanise kunotaura zvokunyaradza kune vose vakasangana nedambudziko iri .
Mumwe mugari wemuTynwald North , Amai Gertrude Magwaniza , vanoti vane hama yavo inogara kuChimanimani iri kutodawo mishonga yavanorarama nayo sezvo yavaive nayo yakayeredzwa nemvura yakasiya yaparadza kumabvazuva kwenyika .
Cyclone Idai yakatanga musi wa 14 Kurume ikasiya yaparadzawo misha nehupenyu hwevanhu muMalawi neMozambique .
Sangano reWorld Health Organization rinoti vanhu vanosvika zana nemakumi mana vafa nechirwere chekorera kuMozambique .
Studio7 haina kukwanisa kunzwa divi regurukota rezvehutano , Va Obediah Moyo , kuti vachaita seyi padambudziko rehutano hwevanhu vari kuChimanimani neChipinge .
Sangano reWOZA neChitatu rakaratidzira muHarare richishora mabatirwo ari kuitwa vari kutengesa mumigwagwa .
Sangano iri rakaendesa tsamba yenyunyuto kugurukota rezvekutongwa kwematunhu VaSaviour Kasukuwere .
Hurumende inoti makanzuru ose emunyika anofanira kudzinga vose vanotengesa zvinhu mumigwagwa .
Asi vanotengesa mumigwagwa ava vanoti havana kugadzirirwa nzvimbo itsva dzekutengesera zvinhu zvavo .
Imwe nhengo yeWOZA muzvare Taurai Nyamanhindi vekuChitungwiza vanoti zvinonetsa ndezvekuti vazhinji vari kutarisana nedambudziko iri madzimai vamwe vavo vakatotadza kuendesa vana kuzvikoro mushure mekushaya mari .
Muzvare Nyamanhindi vanoti kunyangwe zvazvo vasina kuwana mukana wekusangana naVaKasukuwere vari kufara nekuti dzimwe nhengo dzavo dzakakwanisa kusiya tsamba yenyunyuto kuhofisi yavo .
Parizvino veruzhinji vanoita zvekutengesa mumigwagwa vanonzi vari kunonga svosve nemuromo izvo zvatsinirwa naMuzvare Nyamanhindi .
Zviuru nezviuru zvevanhu zvakabviswa mumigwgwa nemapurisa ekanzuru asi vamwe vevanhu ava vari kuramba vachiita hwagonzo nakiti nemapurisa ekanzuruaya sezvo vari kuti havana mabasa .
Nyaya yekusamira zvakanaka kwehupfumi hwenyika ndiyo yapa kuti vanhu vakawanda vagume vaita basa rekutengesa zvinhu mumigwagwa .
Asi vemabhizimisi vanoti vanhu ava vari kuvakanganisa mabasa ravo vachiti vanotambira danho rekuvabvisa mumigwagwa
Chikwata chema Warriors chabudirira kuenderera mberi negadziriro yacho yemutambo wacho neDemocratic Republic of the Congo mugadziriro yachaita neMugovera manheru .
Chikwata ichi chinonzi chaitira gadziriro yacho munhandare yeNadi Sikha Al Hadid muCairo kuEgypt , uko kuri kuitirwa mitambo yeAfcon gore rino .
Vakomana ava vapinda munhandare iyi nenguva dzechinomwe manheru eMugovera , vachikusvidzirwa nezvizvarwa zveZimbabwe zviri muCairo .
Kunyange hazvo pakamboita mitauro yekusabhadharwa kwevatambi ava vachiti vacharamwa kutamba kana vasina kupihwa mari dzavo , vari kuziva zviri kuitika vaudza Studio7 kuti chikwata chemaWarriors chiri munhaurirano nevakuru veZifa panguva iyo vanenge vachigadzirira mutambo wavo wakakosha neDemocratic Republic of the Congo .
Studio7 haina kukwanisa kunzwa kumutungamiri weZifa , VaFelton Kamambo , sezvo tatadza kuvabata parunhare rwavo kuCairo kwavari .
